Your taxable income is your gross pay minus any tax-deductible expenses, such as retirement contributions or health savings account contributions. Your tax rate is the percentage of your taxable income that you pay in taxes. The tax rate varies based on your filing status, income level, and other factors. Let's assume you are single and have a tax rate of 25%.\nTax Rate = 0.25 (25%)\n3. Now, let's calculate your tax liability. (1344, " Great, let's solve this puzzle together! Here's the problem:\nA bowl contains 4.0 red chips, 3.0 blue chips, and 9.0 green chips. You choose 1.0 chip at random. What is the probability that your chip is not red?\nTo solve this problem, we need to use our knowledge of probability and combinatorics. Let's break it down into smaller pieces and calculate each piece separately:\nPiece 1: Red chips\nThe bowl contains 4.0 red chips, which means there are 4.0 possible choices for the red chip.\nProbability of choosing a red chip = 4.0/12.0 = 1/3.0\nPiece 2: Blue chips\nThe bowl contains 3.0 blue chips, which means there are 3.0 possible choices for the blue chip.\nProbability of choosing a blue chip = 3.0/12.0 = 1/4.0\nPiece 3: Green chips\nThe bowl contains 9.0 green chips, which means there are 9.0 possible choices for the green chip.\nProbability of choosing a green chip = 9.0/12.0 = 3/4.0\nPiece 4: Not red\nSince we are choosing 1.0 chip at random, the probability of choosing a red chip is 1/3.0.\nProbability of choosing a chip that is not red = 1 - 1/3.0 = 2/3.0\nNow, let's combine all the pieces to find the final answer:\nProbability of choosing a chip that is not red = 1 - (1/3.0 + 1/4.0 + 3/4.0) = 2/3.0\nSo, the probability")
